type FullName {
  firstName: String!
  lastName: String!
}

"""A workspace member"""
type WorkspaceMember {
  """Id"""
  id: UUID!

  """Workspace member name"""
  name: FullName!

  """Related user email address"""
  userEmail: String!

  """Preferred color scheme"""
  colorScheme: String!

  """Workspace member avatar"""
  avatarUrl: String
  avatarToken: String

  """Preferred language"""
  locale: String

  """User time zone"""
  timeZone: String

  """Actual user time zone value, when timezone is set to system"""
  timeZoneSystemValue: String

  """User's preferred date format"""
  dateFormat: WorkspaceMemberDateFormatEnum

  """User's preferred time format"""
  timeFormat: WorkspaceMemberTimeFormatEnum
  roles: [Role!]
  userWorkspaceId: String

  """Member Feedback"""
  memberFeedback: RawJSONScalar

  """Associated User Id"""
  userId: UUID

  """Preferred AI output language"""
  aiOutputlocale: String

  """Workspace member position"""
  position: Position

  """Date when the record was deleted"""
  deletedAt: DateTime

  """Last time the record was changed"""
  updatedAt: DateTime

  """Creation date"""
  createdAt: DateTime

  """Field used for full-text search"""
  searchVector: String

  """Chat message count"""
  chatMessageCount: Float

  """Workflow members linked to the workspace member"""
  workflowMembers(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: WorkflowMemberFilterInput, orderBy: [WorkflowMemberOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): WorkflowMemberConnection

  """Charts"""
  charts(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: ChartFilterInput, orderBy: [ChartOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): ChartConnection

  """Analytics"""
  dashboards(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: AnalyticDashboardFilterInput, orderBy: [AnalyticDashboardOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): AnalyticDashboardConnection

  """Notification Settings"""
  notificationSetting(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: NotificationSettingFilterInput, orderBy: [NotificationSettingOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): NotificationSettingConnection

  """Device activities linked to the workspace member"""
  deviceActivities(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: DeviceActivityFilterInput, orderBy: [DeviceActivityOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): DeviceActivityConnection

  """Audit Logs linked to the workspace member"""
  auditLogs(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: AuditLogFilterInput, orderBy: [AuditLogOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): AuditLogConnection

  """Events linked to the workspace member"""
  timelineActivities(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: TimelineActivityFilterInput, orderBy: [TimelineActivityOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): TimelineActivityConnection

  """Calendar Event Participants"""
  calendarEventParticipants(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: CalendarEventParticipantFilterInput, orderBy: [CalendarEventParticipantOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): CalendarEventParticipantConnection

  """Blocklisted handles"""
  blocklist(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: BlocklistFilterInput, orderBy: [BlocklistOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): BlocklistConnection

  """Message Participants"""
  messageParticipants(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: MessageParticipantFilterInput, orderBy: [MessageParticipantOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): MessageParticipantConnection

  """Connected accounts"""
  connectedAccounts(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: ConnectedAccountFilterInput, orderBy: [ConnectedAccountOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): ConnectedAccountConnection

  """Attachments created by the workspace member"""
  authoredAttachments(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: AttachmentFilterInput, orderBy: [AttachmentOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): AttachmentConnection

  """Owner for opportunities"""
  ownerForOpportunities(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: OpportunityFilterInput, orderBy: [OpportunityOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): OpportunityConnection

  """Owner for people"""
  ownerForPeople(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: PersonFilterInput, orderBy: [PersonOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): PersonConnection

  """Account owner for companies"""
  accountOwnerForCompanies(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: CompanyFilterInput, orderBy: [CompanyOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): CompanyConnection

  """Favorites linked to the workspace member"""
  favorites(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: FavoriteFilterInput, orderBy: [FavoriteOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): FavoriteConnection

  """Tasks assigned to the workspace member"""
  assignedTasks(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: TaskFilterInput, orderBy: [TaskOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): TaskConnection
}

"""User's preferred date format"""
enum WorkspaceMemberDateFormatEnum {
  """System"""
  SYSTEM

  """Month First"""
  MONTH_FIRST

  """Day First"""
  DAY_FIRST

  """Year First"""
  YEAR_FIRST
}

"""User's preferred time format"""
enum WorkspaceMemberTimeFormatEnum {
  """System"""
  SYSTEM

  """24HRS"""
  HOUR_24

  """12HRS"""
  HOUR_12
}

"""
The `RawJSONScalar` scalar type represents JSON values, but stringifies inputs and parses outputs.
"""
scalar RawJSONScalar

type User {
  id: UUID!
  firstName: String!
  lastName: String!

  defaultAvatarUrl: String

  deletedAt: DateTime

  workspaces: [UserWorkspace!]!
  onboardingStatus: OnboardingStatus
  currentWorkspace: Workspace
  currentUserWorkspace: UserWorkspace
  userVars: JSONObject!
  workspaceMembers: [WorkspaceMember!]
  supportUserHash: String
}

  id: UUID!
  fieldMetadataId: UUID!
  order: Float!

}

type Index {
  id: UUID!
  name: String!
  isCustom: Boolean
  isUnique: Boolean!
  indexWhereClause: String
  indexType: IndexType!
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  objectMetadata(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 10}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: ObjectFilter! = {}
  ): IndexObjectMetadataConnection!
  indexFieldMetadatas(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 10}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: IndexFieldFilter! = {}
  ): IndexIndexFieldMetadatasConnection!
}

"""Type of the index"""
enum IndexType {
  BTREE
  GIN
}

input CursorPaging {
  """Paginate before opaque cursor"""
  before: ConnectionCursor

  """Paginate after opaque cursor"""
  after: ConnectionCursor

  """Paginate first"""
  first: Int

  """Paginate last"""
  last: Int
}

"""Cursor for paging through collections"""
scalar ConnectionCursor

input ObjectFilter {
  and: [ObjectFilter!]
  or: [ObjectFilter!]
  id: UUIDFilterComparison
  isCustom: BooleanFieldComparison
  isRemote: BooleanFieldComparison
  isActive: BooleanFieldComparison
  isSystem: BooleanFieldComparison
  isSearchable: BooleanFieldComparison
}

input UUIDFilterComparison {
  is: Boolean
  isNot: Boolean
  eq: UUID
  neq: UUID
  gt: UUID
  gte: UUID
  lt: UUID
  lte: UUID
  like: UUID
  notLike: UUID
  iLike: UUID
  notILike: UUID
  in: [UUID!]
  notIn: [UUID!]
}

input BooleanFieldComparison {
  is: Boolean
  isNot: Boolean
}

input IndexFieldFilter {
  and: [IndexFieldFilter!]
  or: [IndexFieldFilter!]
  id: UUIDFilterComparison
  fieldMetadataId: UUIDFilterComparison
}

type Object {
  id: UUID!
  dataSourceId: String!
  standardId: String
  nameSingular: String!
  namePlural: String!
  labelSingular: String!
  labelPlural: String!
  description: String
  icon: String
  standardOverrides: ObjectStandardOverrides
  shortcut: String
  isCustom: Boolean!
  isRemote: Boolean!
  isActive: Boolean!
  isSystem: Boolean!
  isSearchable: Boolean!
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  labelIdentifierFieldMetadataId: String
  imageIdentifierFieldMetadataId: String
  isLabelSyncedWithName: Boolean!
  duplicateCriteria: [[String!]!]
  fieldsList: [Field!]!
  fields(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 30}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: FieldFilter! = {}
  ): ObjectFieldsConnection!
  indexMetadatas(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 10}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: IndexFilter! = {}
  ): ObjectIndexMetadatasConnection!
}

input FieldFilter {
  and: [FieldFilter!]
  or: [FieldFilter!]
  id: UUIDFilterComparison
  isCustom: BooleanFieldComparison
  isActive: BooleanFieldComparison
  isVisible: BooleanFieldComparison
  recordOrder: NumberFieldComparison
  isSystem: BooleanFieldComparison
}

input NumberFieldComparison {
  is: Boolean
  isNot: Boolean
  eq: Float
  neq: Float
  gt: Float
  gte: Float
  lt: Float
  lte: Float
  in: [Float!]
  notIn: [Float!]
  between: NumberFieldComparisonBetween
  notBetween: NumberFieldComparisonBetween
}

input NumberFieldComparisonBetween {
  lower: Float!
  upper: Float!
}

input IndexFilter {
  and: [IndexFilter!]
  or: [IndexFilter!]
  id: UUIDFilterComparison
  isCustom: BooleanFieldComparison
}

type RelationMetadata {
  id: UUID!
  relationType: RelationMetadataType!
  fromObjectMetadataId: UUID
  toObjectMetadataId: UUID
  fromPipelineId: UUID
  toPipelineId: UUID
  fromFieldMetadataId: UUID!
  toFieldMetadataId: UUID!
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  fromObjectMetadata: Object!
  toObjectMetadata: Object!
}

"""Type of the relation"""
enum RelationMetadataType {
  ONE_TO_ONE
  ONE_TO_MANY
  MANY_TO_ONE
  MANY_TO_MANY
}

type Field {
  id: UUID!
  type: FieldMetadataType!
  name: String!
  label: String!
  description: String
  icon: String
  standardOverrides: StandardOverrides
  isCustom: Boolean
  isActive: Boolean
  isVisible: Boolean
  recordOrder: Float
  isSystem: Boolean
  isNullable: Boolean
  isUnique: Boolean
  defaultValue: JSON
  options: JSON
  settings: JSON
  objectMetadataId: UUID
  pipelineId: UUID
  statusReasonFieldId: UUID
  isLabelSyncedWithName: Boolean
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  relationDefinition: RelationDefinition
  relation: Relation
  toRelationMetadata: RelationMetadata
  fromRelationMetadata: RelationMetadata
  object: Object
}

"""Type of the field"""
enum FieldMetadataType {
  UUID
  TEXT
  PHONES
  EMAILS
  DATE_TIME
  DATE
  BOOLEAN
  NUMBER
  NUMERIC
  LINKS
  CURRENCY
  FULL_NAME
  RATING
  SELECT
  STATUS
  MULTI_SELECT
  RELATION
  POSITION
  ADDRESS
  RAW_JSON
  RICH_TEXT
  RICH_TEXT_V2
  ACTOR
  ARRAY
  TS_VECTOR
  MORPH_RELATION
}

type RelationDefinition {
  relationId: UUID!
  sourceObjectMetadata: Object!
  targetObjectMetadata: Object!
  sourceFieldMetadata: Field!
  targetFieldMetadata: Field!
  direction: RelationDefinitionType!
}

"""Relation definition type"""
enum RelationDefinitionType {
  ONE_TO_ONE
  ONE_TO_MANY
  MANY_TO_MANY
  MANY_TO_ONE
}

type IndexEdge {
  """The node containing the Index"""
  node: Index!

  """Cursor for this node."""
  cursor: ConnectionCursor!
}

type PageInfo {
  """true if paging forward and there are more records."""
  hasNextPage: Boolean!

  """true if paging backwards and there are more records."""
  hasPreviousPage: Boolean!

  """The cursor of the first returned record."""
  startCursor: ConnectionCursor

  """The cursor of the last returned record."""
  endCursor: ConnectionCursor
}

type IndexConnection {
  """Paging information"""
  pageInfo: PageInfo!

  """Array of edges."""
  edges: [IndexEdge!]!
}

type IndexFieldEdge {
  """The node containing the IndexField"""
  node: IndexField!

  """Cursor for this node."""
  cursor: ConnectionCursor!
}

type IndexIndexFieldMetadatasConnection {
  """Paging information"""
  pageInfo: PageInfo!

  """Array of edges."""
  edges: [IndexFieldEdge!]!
}

type ObjectEdge {
  """The node containing the Object"""
  node: Object!

  """Cursor for this node."""
  cursor: ConnectionCursor!
}

type IndexObjectMetadataConnection {
  """Paging information"""
  pageInfo: PageInfo!

  """Array of edges."""
  edges: [ObjectEdge!]!
}

type Pipeline {
  id: UUID!
  objectMetadataId: String!
  standardId: String
  dataSourceId: String!
  nameSingular: String!
  namePlural: String!
  labelSingular: String!
  labelPlural: String!
  description: String
  icon: String
  standardOverrides: PipelineStandardOverrides
  targetTableName: String!
  isCustom: Boolean!
  isRemote: Boolean!
  isActive: Boolean!
  isSystem: Boolean!
  isAuditLogged: Boolean!
  isLabelSyncedWithName: Boolean!
  isSearchable: Boolean!
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  objectMetadata: Object!
  templateId: String
  fields(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 30}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: FieldFilter! = {}
  ): PipelineFieldsConnection!
  indexMetadatas(
    """Limit or page results."""
    paging: CursorPaging! = {first: 10}

    """Specify to filter the records returned."""
    filter: IndexFilter! = {}
  ): PipelineIndexMetadatasConnection!
}

"""A workflow run"""
type WorkflowRun {
  workflowRunId: UUID!

  """Workflow run ended at"""
  endedAt: DateTime

  """Workflow run started at"""
  startedAt: DateTime

  """Workflow run enqueued at"""
  enqueuedAt: DateTime

  """Name of the workflow run"""
  name: String

  """Workflow linked to the run. id foreign key"""
  workflowId: UUID

  """Workflow version linked to the run. id foreign key"""
  workflowVersionId: UUID

  """Date when the record was deleted"""
  deletedAt: DateTime

  """Last time the record was changed"""
  updatedAt: DateTime

  """Creation date"""
  createdAt: DateTime

  """Id"""
  id: UUID

  """Field used for full-text search"""
  searchVector: String

  """Workflow run position"""
  position: Position

  """State of the workflow run"""
  state: RawJSONScalar

  """The executor of the workflow"""
  createdBy: Actor

  """Workflow run status"""
  status: WorkflowRunStatusEnum

  """Timeline activities linked to the run"""
  timelineActivities(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: TimelineActivityFilterInput, orderBy: [TimelineActivityOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): TimelineActivityConnection

  """Favorites linked to the workflow run"""
  favorites(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: FavoriteFilterInput, orderBy: [FavoriteOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): FavoriteConnection

  """Workflow linked to the run."""
  workflow: Workflow

  """Workflow version linked to the run."""
  workflowVersion: WorkflowVersion
}

  stepsDiff: JSON

input GroupFilterInput {
  id: String
  name: String
  parentGroupId: String
  isAllCompany: Boolean
  workspaceId: String
}

input GroupPaginationInput {
  skip: Int! = 0
  take: Int! = 20
}

input UserWorkspaceFilterInput {
  isActive: Boolean
  email: String
  name: String
  roleType: String
  skip: Int
  take: Int
}

input ServerlessFunctionIdInput {
  """The id of the function."""
  id: ID!
}

input GetServerlessFunctionSourceCodeInput {
  """The id of the function."""
  id: ID!

  """The version of the function"""
  version: String! = "draft"
}

union UserExistsOutput = UserExists | UserNotExists

type UserExists {
  exists: Boolean!
  availableWorkspaces: [AvailableWorkspaceOutput!]!
  isEmailVerified: Boolean!
}

type UserNotExists {
  exists: Boolean!
}

input ReportingQueryInput {
  objectNameSingular: String!
  selectFields: [String!]
  groupBy: [GroupByField!]
  aggregations: [AggregationField!]
  filters: [FilterCondition!]
  sorting: [SortField!]
  chartType: ChartType! = TABLE
  limit: Float
  offset: Float
  comparisonDates: [FilterCondition!]
  isHistoricChart: Boolean = false
  dateGrouping: String
  isNonCumulative: Boolean = false
}

input GroupByField {
  field: String!
  alias: String
  type: FieldMetadataType
  options: [String!]
}

input AggregationField {
  field: String!
  function: AggregateOperations!
  alias: String
}

enum AggregateOperations {
  min
  max
  avg
  sum
  count
  countUniqueValues
  countEmpty
  countNotEmpty
  countTrue
  countFalse
  percentageEmpty
  percentageNotEmpty
}

input FilterCondition {
  field: String!
  operator: String!
  value: String
  values: [String!]
}

input SortField {
  field: String!
  direction: SortDirection! = ASC
}

"""Sort direction (ascending or descending)"""
enum SortDirection {
  ASC
  DESC
}

input ObjectRecordFilterInput {
  and: [ObjectRecordFilterInput!]
  not: ObjectRecordFilterInput
  or: [ObjectRecordFilterInput!]
  id: UUIDFilter
  createdAt: DateFilter
  updatedAt: DateFilter
  deletedAt: DateFilter
}

input UUIDFilter {
  eq: UUID
  gt: UUID
  gte: UUID
  in: [UUID!]
  lt: UUID
  lte: UUID
  neq: UUID
  is: FilterIs
}

"""This enum to filter by nullability"""
enum FilterIs {
  """Nulish values"""
  NULL

  """Non-nulish values"""
  NOT_NULL
  NotNull
  Null
}

input DateFilter {
  eq: Date
  gt: Date
  gte: Date
  in: [Date!]
  lt: Date
  lte: Date
  neq: Date
  is: FilterIs
}

"""Date custom scalar type"""
scalar Date

"""A Meeting note"""
type AiMeetingNote {
  """Date when the record was deleted"""
  deletedAt: DateTime

  """Last time the record was changed"""
  updatedAt: DateTime

  """Creation date"""
  createdAt: DateTime

  """Id"""
  id: UUID

  """Field used for full-text search"""
  searchVector: String

  """Calendar Invitees"""
  calendarInvitees: RawJSONScalar

  """The creator of the record"""
  createdBy: Actor

  """Group ID for visibility"""
  groupId: UUID

  """Record visibility level"""
  visibilityLevel: Float

  """Share URL"""
  shareUrl: Links

  """Transcript Language"""
  transcriptLanguage: String

  """Meeting Action Items"""
  actionItems: RawJSONScalar

  """Recording Id"""
  recordingId: String

  """Meeting Summary"""
  summary: String

  """Meeting Note Title"""
  title: String

  """Favorites linked to the AI Meeting Note"""
  favorites(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: FavoriteFilterInput, orderBy: [FavoriteOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): FavoriteConnection

  """Timeline Activities linked to the task."""
  timelineActivities(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: TimelineActivityFilterInput, orderBy: [TimelineActivityOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): TimelineActivityConnection

  """AI Meeting Note Participants"""
  aiMeetingNoteParticipants(first: Int, last: Int, before: String, after: String, limit: Int, filter: AiMeetingNoteParticipantFilterInput, orderBy: [AiMeetingNoteParticipantOrderByInput], fetchAll: Boolean): AiMeetingNoteParticipantConnection
}

  """Message Participants"""

  """Message Thread Id"""

  """"""
  description: String

  """Webhook operations"""
  operations: [String]

  """Webhook target url"""
  targetUrl: String
}

"""Records shared with other users"""
type SharedRecord {
  """Date when the record was deleted"""
  deletedAt: DateTime

  """Last time the record was changed"""
  updatedAt: DateTime

  """Creation date"""
  createdAt: DateTime

  """Id"""
  id: UUID

  """Whether the user can share the record"""
  canShare: Boolean

  """Whether the user can delete the record"""
  canDelete: Boolean

  """Whether the user can edit the record"""
  canEdit: Boolean

  """Whether the sharing is active"""
  isActive: Boolean

  """The date and time when the sharing expires"""
  expiresAt: DateTime

  """The ID of the user workspace the record is shared with"""
  sharedWithWorkspaceMemberId: UUID

  """The ID of the user workspace that shared the record"""
  sharedByWorkspaceMemberId: UUID

  """The ID of the object metadata"""
  objectMetadataId: UUID

  """The ID of the shared record"""
  recordId: UUID
}

"""A score history record"""

  """Last time the record was changed"""

  """Creation date"""

}

"""A pending score event for debouncing"""

  """The record identifier"""

}

"""A list for gg"""

  recordId: UUID

  updatedAt: DateTime

  """Reasons for stage"""

  """Parent opportunity object"""
  parent: Opportunity
}

  """Stage 1"""
  STAGE_1

  """Stage 2"""
  STAGE_2

  """Stage 3"""
  STAGE_3

  """Stage 4"""
  STAGE_4

  """Stage 5"""
  STAGE_5
}

"""Reasons for stage"""
enum GgReasonsForStageEnum {
  """There has been no response from the customer"""
  THERE_HAS_BEEN_NO_RE
}

  eq: String

  lte: String

"""This enum is used to specify the order of results"""
enum OrderByDirection {
  """Ascending order, nulls first"""
  AscNullsFirst

  """Ascending order, nulls last"""
  AscNullsLast

  """Descending order, nulls first"""
  DescNullsFirst

  """Descending order, nulls last"""
  DescNullsLast
}
